CIS_IDLE
  0C IP_WAIT -> RX_WAIT
  Send 0 bit

CIS_RX_WAIT
Send done -> CIS_IDLE

CIS_IDLE
  IP_OPEN_WR ->CIS_WAIT_2

CIS_WAIT_2
  IP_READ_STATUS -> CIS_WAIT_3 and send bit 1
